                Roy Cho, alleged mastermind of Hong Kong’s biggest fraud case, denies fresh charge of deceiving staff at Convoy as trial gets under way
            </h1><div class="info__subHeadline" data-v-3c0c8cda><div data-v-3c0c8cda><ul class="generic-article__summary--ul content--ul" data-v-c100079c data-v-3c0c8cda>
<li class="generic-article__summary--li content--li" data-v-c100079c>Trial begins of former Convoy executive director, Roy Cho kwai-chee, the alleged mastermind of Hong Kong’s largest financial investigation in decades</li>
